                      <div dir="ltr" class="_5wjy">
                       <p>Boolean logic: not always so logical.</p>
                      </div>

                        <div id="u_0_1f" class="_6m2 _1zpr clearfix _dcs _4_w4 _5cwb _5qqr" data-ft="{&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;H&quot;}">

                             <div class="_6m3">
                              <div dir="ltr" class="_5wjy mbs _6m6 _2cnj">
                               <a href="http://l.facebook.com/l.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fstackoverflow.com%2Fquestions%2F31421379%2Fwhy-does-nottrue-in-false-true-return-false%3Futm_medium%3Dsocial%26utm_source%3Dfacebook.com%26utm_campaign%3Dso-facebook&amp;h=hAQE_lKxc&amp;enc=AZM5W4pejMiwcrPrexsd8_DMbwNSAzOaBjxocMaQoGwHaJCEiukhr1wi7cznWPEXoJbPy7yZcd0Ay-R2_nwjxFOTprFXctL1PIc4R62lQwmtAEXP1DZINWhLwcK7KctguvIUB0tWNpEf_Xo1eElDJNIlbNsmCFnaqwaDdKwS93P6N1dyDq6RCbShn0uCoVIuyIBiGgS6c7SakppN5ngxfWpz&amp;s=1" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" onmouseover="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\/\/stackoverflow.com\/questions\/31421379\/why-does-nottrue-in-false-true-return-false?utm_medium=social&amp;utm_source=facebook.com&amp;utm_campaign=so-facebook&quot;);" onclick="LinkshimAsyncLink.swap(this, &quot;http:\/\/l.facebook.com\/l.php?u=http\u00253A\u00252F\u00252Fstackoverflow.com\u00252Fquestions\u00252F31421379\u00252Fwhy-does-nottrue-in-false-true-return-false\u00253Futm_medium\u00253Dsocial\u002526utm_source\u00253Dfacebook.com\u002526utm_campaign\u00253Dso-facebook&amp;h=hAQE_lKxc&amp;enc=AZM5W4pejMiwcrPrexsd8_DMbwNSAzOaBjxocMaQoGwHaJCEiukhr1wi7cznWPEXoJbPy7yZcd0Ay-R2_nwjxFOTprFXctL1PIc4R62lQwmtAEXP1DZINWhLwcK7KctguvIUB0tWNpEf_Xo1eElDJNIlbNsmCFnaqwaDdKwS93P6N1dyDq6RCbShn0uCoVIuyIBiGgS6c7SakppN5ngxfWpz&amp;s=1&quot;);">Why does "not(True) in [False, True]" return False?</a>
                              </div>
                              <div class="_5wjy _6m7 _3bt9">
                               <span dir="ltr">If I do that: &gt;&gt;&gt; False in [False, True] True That return True. Simply because False is in the list... But if I do: &gt;&gt;&gt; not(True) in [False, True] False That return False.</span>
                              </div>
